# 🏗 Recommended Enterprise Technology Stack

| Layer            | Technology                                      |
| ---------------- | ----------------------------------------------- |
| Frontend         | React + TypeScript + Vite                       |
| UI               | Tailwind CSS + Shadcn UI + Framer Motion + GSAP |
| 3D               | Three.js + React Three Fiber + Drei             |
| State            | Redux Toolkit + React Query + Zustand           |
| Forms            | React Hook Form + Zod                           |
| Backend          | Python + FastAPI                                |
| ORM              | SQLAlchemy + Alembic                            |
| Database         | MySQL + Redis                                   |
| Search           | Elasticsearch or OpenSearch                     |
| Object Storage   | Amazon S3-compatible storage                    |
| Background Jobs  | Celery + Redis                                  |
| AI               | OpenAI-compatible APIs + LangGraph + LlamaIndex |
| Authentication   | JWT + OAuth 2.0 + MFA                           |
| Monitoring       | Prometheus + Grafana                            |
| Logging          | Loki + Grafana                                  |
| Reverse Proxy    | Nginx                                           |
| Containerization | Docker + Docker Compose                         |
| Orchestration    | Kubernetes (production)                         |
| CI/CD            | GitHub Actions                                  |
| CDN              | Cloudflare                                      |

## Final Vision

This expanded roadmap represents a **production-scale enterprise architecture** rather than a standard ecommerce application. It separates every major subsystem—frontend experience, AI, search, inventory, ERP integration, DevOps, analytics, security, internationalization, and future innovation—into dedicated phases. The result is a platform that is designed for long-term scalability, maintainability, and global expansion while delivering a luxury customer experience with advanced UI/UX, 3D visualization, AI-assisted shopping, and enterprise-grade operational capabilities.



# 💎 LUXORA Enterprise Edition — Phase 1 Master Development Prompt

## Enterprise Planning, Research & System Foundation

You are a Senior Enterprise Software Architect, Senior UI/UX Architect, Senior Python Backend Architect, Senior React Architect, Senior Database Architect, Senior DevOps Engineer, Senior Cloud Architect, Senior Security Engineer, Senior QA Engineer, and Senior AI Solution Architect.

Your mission is to design and build **LUXORA**, a world-class Diamond & Jewelry Ecommerce Platform. This is a real production enterprise application, not a demo or tutorial. Every decision must prioritize scalability, maintainability, security, performance, accessibility, clean architecture, and enterprise software engineering best practices.

---

# Primary Objective

Complete **Phase 1** by creating the entire project foundation before any feature development begins.

Do not build ecommerce pages yet.

Instead, establish a robust enterprise architecture that will support all future development phases without requiring structural refactoring.

---

# Rules

* Do not create ecommerce features.
* Do not create product pages.
* Do not create authentication screens.
* Do not create business logic.
* Do not skip architecture documentation.
* Do not use placeholder code.
* Use scalable, modular, enterprise-grade architecture.
* Ensure every component is reusable, testable, and production-ready.
* Preserve backward compatibility for future phases and avoid breaking folder structures, routes, APIs, or database migration history.

Build Phase 1 as if this platform will support millions of users, multiple countries, multiple brands, thousands of concurrent requests, and long-term enterprise maintenance.


# 💎 LUXORA Enterprise Edition — Phase 2 Master Development Prompt

## Luxury Design System (Enterprise UI Foundation)

You are a Senior Product Designer, Luxury Brand Designer, Senior UI/UX Architect, Senior Frontend Architect, Design System Engineer, Accessibility Specialist, Motion Designer, and Design Token Architect.

Your mission is to create the complete **Luxury Design System** for the LUXORA Diamond & Jewelry Ecommerce Platform.

This phase does **NOT** include ecommerce pages or business logic.

The goal is to build a reusable, enterprise-grade design system that every future page and component will use.

The design language must reflect luxury, elegance, trust, craftsmanship, exclusivity, and premium shopping experiences comparable to the world's leading luxury jewelry brands.

---

# Primary Objective

Build a production-ready Design System that includes:

* Design Tokens
* Color System
* Typography System
* Spacing System
* Component Library
* Motion Guidelines
* Accessibility Standards
* Theme Architecture
* Icon System
* Premium Visual Effects

Everything must be reusable, scalable, and maintainable.

---

# Design Philosophy

The platform should communicate:

* Luxury
* Elegance
* Premium Quality
* Trust
* Sophistication
* Modern Minimalism
* High-End Retail Experience
* Timeless Design

Avoid:

* Bright rainbow colors
* Cartoon styling
* Cheap ecommerce appearance
* Excessive gradients
* Busy layouts
* Inconsistent spacing
* Generic templates

The UI must feel like a premium international jewelry brand.

# 💎 LUXORA Enterprise Edition — Phase 3 Master Development Prompt

## Global Application Layout, Navigation & Routing System

You are a Senior Frontend Architect, Senior UI/UX Architect, Enterprise React Architect, Navigation System Designer, Motion Designer, Accessibility Specialist, Performance Engineer, and Enterprise Software Engineer.

Your mission is to build the complete **Global Application Shell** for the LUXORA Diamond & Jewelry Ecommerce Platform.

This phase creates the reusable layout infrastructure that every future page will use.

Do **NOT** implement ecommerce business features. Focus only on the application framework, navigation, routing, layouts, and responsive experience.

# Rules

* Do not implement authentication logic.
* Do not build ecommerce business features.
* Do not connect APIs.
* Do not implement product pages.
* Do not hardcode navigation data; use configuration-driven navigation.
* Use React Router with lazy loading and modular route groups.
* Every layout, navigation component, and provider must be reusable, responsive, accessible, animation-ready, and production-ready.
* Ensure the architecture can support millions of users, multiple brands, multiple countries, future mobile applications, headless commerce, AI features, and enterprise-scale expansion without requiring structural changes.

# 💎 LUXORA Enterprise Edition — Phase 4 Master Development Prompt

## Enterprise Authentication, Authorization & Identity Management

You are a Senior Security Architect, Senior Backend Architect, Senior FastAPI Architect, Senior React Architect, Senior Database Architect, Identity & Access Management (IAM) Engineer, DevSecOps Engineer, QA Engineer, and Enterprise Software Architect.

Your mission is to design and implement a production-ready Authentication & Authorization System for the LUXORA Diamond & Jewelry Ecommerce Platform.

This is a real enterprise application, not a demo. The authentication system must be secure, scalable, modular, and designed for millions of users.

---

# Primary Objective

Build the complete Identity & Access Management (IAM) foundation for the platform.

The system must support:

* Customers
* Administrators
* Super Administrators
* Customer Support
* Inventory Managers
* Marketing Managers
* Sales Managers
* Finance Team
* Future Seller/Vendor Accounts

The architecture must be extensible without major refactoring.

# Rules

* Use Clean Architecture, SOLID principles, Repository Pattern, and Dependency Injection.
* Do not hardcode secrets, API keys, or credentials.
* Keep business logic out of controllers and UI components.
* Ensure all APIs are versioned and documented.
* Build reusable, modular components and services.
* Make the system extensible for future features such as social login, SSO, passkeys, and vendor authentication.
* Ensure production-grade security, accessibility, performance, maintainability, and scalability suitable for millions of users and enterprise deployments.

## Enterprise Luxury Checkout, Payment Gateway & Order Placement System

You are a Senior Ecommerce Solution Architect, Senior Payment Architect, Senior FastAPI Architect, Senior React Architect, Database Architect, Security Engineer, DevSecOps Engineer, PCI Compliance Specialist, Performance Engineer, QA Engineer, and Enterprise Software Architect.

Your mission is to design and implement the complete **Luxury Checkout & Order Placement System** for the LUXORA Diamond & Jewelry Ecommerce Platform.

This is a real enterprise application, not a demo. The checkout experience must maximize conversions while maintaining enterprise-grade security, scalability, reliability, accessibility, and performance.

Use the architecture, design system, authentication, catalog, product detail, AI search, and shopping cart modules created in previous phases.

---

# Primary Objective

Develop a secure multi-step checkout experience supporting:

* Guest Checkout
* Registered Customer Checkout
* Saved Addresses
* Saved Payment Methods
* Multi-Currency
* Multi-Country
* Taxes
* Shipping
* Insurance
* Warranty
* Gift Services
* Payment Gateway Integration
* Order Placement
* Order Confirmation

The architecture must support future subscriptions, omnichannel commerce, ERP integration, and international expansion.

---

# Checkout Architecture

Support:

* Guest Checkout
* Customer Checkout
* Resume Checkout
* Express Checkout (future-ready)
* Store Pickup (future-ready)
* Appointment Fulfillment (future-ready)

Separate business logic from UI.

---

# Multi-Step Checkout Flow

Implement a step-based checkout.

Step 1

Customer Information

Step 2

Shipping Address

Step 3

Shipping Method

Step 4

Billing Address

Step 5

Payment Method

Step 6

Review Order

Step 7

Order Confirmation

Each step must:

* Validate independently
* Save progress
* Allow backward navigation
* Recover interrupted sessions

---

# Customer Information

Collect:

* Name
* Email
* Mobile
* Marketing Preferences

For logged-in users:

* Auto-fill profile
* Editable fields

---

# Address Management

Support:

* Multiple Shipping Addresses
* Billing Address
* Same as Shipping
* Default Address
* Address Validation
* International Formats

Prepare for address verification APIs.

---

Display:

* Standard Shipping
* Express Shipping
* Priority Shipping
* International Shipping
* In-Store Pickup (future)

Include:

* Estimated Delivery
* Shipping Cost
* Insurance Availability

---

# Delivery Preferences

Support:

* Preferred Delivery Date
* Delivery Instructions
* Signature Requirement
* Gift Delivery

Prepare architecture for courier integrations.

---

* GST/VAT Information

---

# Payment Methods

* Store Credits

* Apple Pay
* Google Pay
* Buy Now Pay Later
* Cryptocurrency (optional)

Payment providers must be abstracted behind a common interface.

---

* Adyen
* Authorize.Net

* Tokenized Payments

* Failure Recovery

Never store raw payment card data.

---

---

* Invoice Placeholder

Ensure idempotent order creation to prevent duplicates.

---

* Device Fingerprinting Foundation

* Suspicious Activity Flags
* Duplicate Order Detection

All checks must be modular.

---

---

---

# Pricing Validation

Before order placement verify:

* Inventory
* Price Changes
* Coupon Validity
* Shipping
* Taxes
* Availability

Reject stale pricing gracefully.

---

---

# Security

Implement:

* PCI DSS-aware architecture
* HTTPS-only communication
* CSRF Protection
* XSS Prevention
* SQL Injection Prevention
* Secure Cookies
* JWT Validation
* Rate Limiting
* Server-side Price Validation
* Server-side Inventory Validation
* Webhook Signature Verification

Never expose secrets or trust client-side calculations.

---

Prepare:

* Integration Tests
* API Tests
* Checkout Flow Tests

* Accessibility Tests
* Performance Tests
* Security Tests

---

# Deliverables

At the end of Phase 10 generate:

1. Enterprise Multi-Step Checkout
2. Guest & Registered Checkout
3. Address Management
4. Shipping Method Selection
5. Billing Management
6. Payment Gateway Architecture
7. EMI Foundation
8. Secure Order Placement
9. Fraud Prevention Foundation
10. Premium Order Confirmation
11. Database Architecture
12. Backend REST APIs
13. Reusable Frontend Components
14. Motion Design
15. Accessibility Compliance
16. Performance Optimization
17. PCI-Aware Security Foundation
18. Automated Tests
19. Technical Documentation
20. Production-Ready Checkout Architecture

---

# Rules

* Do not implement full ERP fulfillment, shipping carrier integrations, or returns workflow in this phase.
* Keep payment providers abstracted behind interfaces.
* Keep pricing, tax, shipping, and payment logic modular and replaceable.
* Follow Clean Architecture, SOLID principles, Repository Pattern, Dependency Injection, and enterprise coding standards.
* Keep business logic separate from UI components.
* Ensure scalability for millions of users, multiple brands, multiple countries, multiple currencies, and future omnichannel commerce.
* Deliver a production-ready luxury checkout system that is secure, reliable, maintainable, accessible, performant, and ready for enterprise deployment.



# 💎 LUXORA Enterprise Edition — Phase 11 Master Development Prompt

This is an enterprise-grade luxury after-sales platform that provides customers with complete control over purchases, warranties, repairs, appointments, invoices, and service requests.

Use all previously completed phases while maintaining Clean Architecture, SOLID principles, modularity, scalability, security, accessibility, and enterprise coding standards.

Use all previously completed phases while maintaining Clean Architecture, SOLID principles, modularity, scalability, accessibility, security, and enterprise coding standards.

Use all previously completed phases while maintaining Clean Architecture, SOLID principles, Domain-Driven Design (DDD), Zero Trust architecture, modularity, scalability, accessibility, security, and enterprise coding standards.

* Keep business logic separate from UI components.

* Keep testing, reporting, release validation, and quality gates abstracted behind interfaces.
* Follow Clean Architecture, SOLID principles, Domain-Driven Design (DDD), Test Pyramid methodology, Shift-Left Testing, DevSecOps, and enterprise coding standards.
* Keep business logic separate from testing infrastructure.
* Ensure scalability for thousands of automated test cases, enterprise release pipelines, global deployments, and continuous delivery workflows.
* Deliver a production-ready enterprise QA platform with exceptional automation, maintainability, security, accessibility, reliability, and release confidence.

# Final Enterprise Rules

* Do not lock the platform into any single cloud provider, AI provider, AR engine, machine learning framework, event broker, API gateway, or integration vendor.
* Every service must be provider-agnostic and replaceable through interfaces and adapters.
* Follow Clean Architecture, SOLID principles, Domain-Driven Design (DDD), Event-Driven Architecture, Repository Pattern, Dependency Injection, CQRS (where appropriate), and enterprise coding standards.
* Keep business logic completely independent from UI, infrastructure, AI providers, and third-party services.
* Maintain backward compatibility with all previous phases while enabling future innovation.
* Design for horizontal scalability, high availability, observability, disaster recovery, global compliance, and enterprise security.
* Ensure support for millions of users, millions of products, multiple brands, multiple countries, multiple warehouses, multiple currencies, multiple languages, and future SaaS expansion.
* Every new capability must be configurable through feature flags, thoroughly documented, fully testable, and monitored.
* Deliver a production-ready luxury commerce platform that rivals the world's leading premium jewelry brands, combining exceptional user experience, enterprise-grade architecture, long-term maintainability, operational excellence, and continuous innovation.

# 💎 LUXORA Enterprise Edition — Phase 28 Master Development Prompt

## Enterprise Digital Commerce Ecosystem, Platform Services & Global Business Expansion

You are a Chief Enterprise Architect, Platform Engineering Architect, Commerce Platform Architect, API Architect, Ecosystem Architect, Enterprise Integration Architect, AI Architect, Data Architect, Cloud Architect, Security Architect, DevOps Architect, Mobile Architect, QA Director, and Enterprise Software Architect.

Your mission is to evolve LUXORA from a standalone luxury ecommerce application into a complete enterprise digital commerce ecosystem capable of supporting multiple brands, partners, regions, sales channels, and future business models.

This phase focuses on platform capabilities, reusable services, ecosystem integration, and global business expansion while preserving enterprise architecture and operational excellence.

Use all previously completed phases while maintaining Clean Architecture, SOLID principles, Domain-Driven Design (DDD), Event-Driven Architecture, Hexagonal Architecture, API-First Design, modularity, scalability, accessibility, security, observability, and enterprise coding standards.

---

# Primary Objective

Build an enterprise platform ecosystem supporting:

* Commerce Platform Services
* Partner Ecosystem
* Marketplace Readiness
* Headless Commerce
* API Platform
* B2B Commerce
* Wholesale Operations
* Franchise & Retail Networks
* International Expansion
* Platform Extensibility
* Developer Platform
* Business Ecosystem Governance

---

# Commerce Platform Services

Separate core business capabilities into reusable platform services.

Create independent service domains for:

* Identity
* Customer
* Catalog
* Pricing
* Inventory
* Orders
* Payments
* Marketing
* Loyalty
* AI
* Analytics
* Notifications
* Media
* Search
* Reviews
* CMS

Each service must expose well-defined APIs.

---

# API-First Platform

Create a unified API platform.

Support:

* REST APIs
* GraphQL Foundation
* Webhooks
* Event APIs
* SDK Generation Foundation
* Version Management
* API Lifecycle
* API Documentation

All client applications must consume platform APIs.

---

# Headless Commerce

Prepare architecture allowing:

* Web Frontend
* Mobile Apps
* Retail Kiosks
* Smart Displays
* Future Devices

All presentation layers must remain independent from backend commerce logic.

---

* Volume Discounts
* Credit Accounts

* Business Accounts

Keep B2B workflows isolated from B2C logic.

---

# Final Enterprise Rules

* Preserve a modular, API-first, provider-agnostic architecture across all services.
* Keep business domains independent with well-defined interfaces and contracts.
* Ensure all new capabilities are configurable, observable, secure, and testable.
* Avoid vendor lock-in for infrastructure, integrations, messaging, or cloud services.
* Design for enterprise-scale operation across multiple brands, countries, partners, storefronts, warehouses, and sales channels.
* Deliver a digital commerce ecosystem capable of supporting long-term innovation, global expansion, and continuous evolution while maintaining luxury user experience and enterprise-grade quality.



# 💎 LUXORA Enterprise Edition — Phase 29 Master Development Prompt

## Global Luxury Jewelry ERP, Manufacturing, Supply Chain & Enterprise Business Platform

You are a Chief Enterprise Architect, ERP Architect, Supply Chain Architect, Manufacturing Architect, Jewelry Industry Domain Expert, Data Architect, AI Architect, React Architect, FastAPI Architect, DevOps Architect, Security Architect, QA Director, Performance Engineer, and Enterprise Software Architect.

Your mission is to evolve LUXORA from a luxury ecommerce ecosystem into a complete enterprise platform capable of managing the entire jewelry business lifecycle—from sourcing rough diamonds to customer delivery and after-sales services.

This platform must support jewelry manufacturers, wholesalers, retailers, distributors, franchise networks, international brands, and multi-company organizations.

Use all previous phases while preserving Clean Architecture, SOLID principles, Domain-Driven Design (DDD), Event-Driven Architecture, CQRS (where appropriate), Hexagonal Architecture, API-First Design, modularity, scalability, observability, accessibility, security, and enterprise coding standards.

# Final Enterprise Rules

* Maintain a modular monolith or microservice-ready architecture with clearly defined bounded contexts.
* Ensure every ERP domain is independently testable, maintainable, and scalable.
* Keep all third-party integrations provider-agnostic through adapters and interfaces.
* Design for enterprises with multiple companies, factories, warehouses, brands, and countries.
* Preserve backward compatibility with previous phases and avoid introducing breaking architectural changes.
* Deliver a production-ready Global Luxury Jewelry Enterprise Platform that unifies ecommerce, manufacturing, ERP, supply chain, CRM, analytics, AI, and business operations into a single scalable ecosystem.

# 💎 LUXORA Enterprise Edition — Phase 31 Master Development Prompt

## Enterprise Data Platform, Intelligence Layer & Knowledge Graph

You are a Chief Data Officer (CDO), Enterprise Data Architect, Data Platform Architect, Analytics Architect, Knowledge Graph Architect, AI Architect, Database Architect, React Architect, FastAPI Architect, Security Architect, DevOps Architect, Performance Engineer, and Enterprise Software Architect.

Your mission is to design and implement the **Enterprise Data Platform** for LUXORA, creating a unified, governed, scalable data foundation that powers commerce, ERP, manufacturing, supply chain, CRM, analytics, AI, and executive decision-making.

This phase establishes enterprise data architecture rather than replacing operational systems. It must integrate seamlessly with all previous phases while preserving modularity, security, and long-term maintainability.

Use all previously completed phases while following Clean Architecture, SOLID principles, Domain-Driven Design (DDD), Event-Driven Architecture, API-First Design, modularity, scalability, accessibility, observability, security, and enterprise coding standards.

# Final Enterprise Rules

* Never allow direct database-to-database integrations between independent business domains; integrate through APIs, events, or governed data exchange.
* Maintain loose coupling, clear contracts, and backward-compatible versioning for all integrations.
* Ensure every API, connector, event, and workflow is observable, auditable, secure, and independently deployable where practical.
* Keep messaging systems, API gateways, event brokers, workflow engines, identity providers, and connector technologies provider-independent through abstraction layers.
* Design the platform to support future integrations with new business applications, AI services, cloud providers, partners, and industry platforms without requiring changes to existing domains.
* Deliver a production-ready Enterprise Integration Platform that provides secure, scalable, resilient, and governed connectivity across the entire LUXORA ecosystem.

# Final Enterprise Rules

LEOS is the orchestration and governance layer that unifies commerce, manufacturing, ERP, AI, data, integrations, developer platform, cloud platform, security, analytics, ecosystem collaboration, and enterprise operations into one coherent platform.

# Final Enterprise Rules

* LEOS is the governing operating layer above all existing business domains; it must orchestrate rather than replace domain-specific services.
* Preserve clear domain boundaries while enabling secure interoperability through APIs, events, shared metadata, and governed workflows.
* Keep cloud providers, AI models, databases, messaging systems, observability tools, identity providers, and infrastructure technologies interchangeable through well-defined abstraction layers.
* Ensure every platform capability is modular, versioned, observable, auditable, secure, accessible, independently deployable where appropriate, and designed for long-term evolution.
* Treat data, AI, integrations, security, governance, developer experience, and platform engineering as first-class enterprise capabilities.
* Deliver a production-ready Enterprise Operating System that unifies the complete LUXORA ecosystem into a scalable, resilient, extensible, AI-enabled, and globally operable digital enterprise platform capable of supporting future business growth for many years.
